U+FF00 全角字符
[U+3000, U+3040/302A) cjk标点符号
[U+FF00, U+FFF0) 半角字符的全角字符


python -c 'print("\u3000")'
'　'
python -c 'print("".join(chr(i) for i in range(0x3000, 0x302A)))' > ~/tmp/全角标点.txt

,(0x3000, 0x3040)
: 'CJK Symbols and Punctuation'
,(0x3200, 0x3300)
: 'Enclosed CJK Letters and Months'
,(0xfe30, 0xfe50)
: 'CJK Compatibility Forms'
,(0xfe50, 0xfe70)
: 'Small Form Variants'
,(0xff00, 0xfff0)
: 'Halfwidth and Fullwidth Forms'
===

for j in range(0x3000, 0x3040):print(hex(j), (chr(j)))

for j in range(0xfe30, 0xfe50):print(hex(j), (chr(j)))

for j in range(0xfe50, 0xfe70):print(hex(j), (chr(j)))

for j in range(0xff00, 0xfff0):print(hex(j), (chr(j)))

import unicodedata as U
>>> U.unidata_version
'14.0.0'

U.ucd_3_2_0

,postal
:邮政的
>>> U.name('〠')
'POSTAL MARK FACE'


>>> U.name('\ufe53')
Traceback (most recent call last):
  ...
ValueError: no such name
>>> U.name('\ufe52')
'SMALL FULL STOP'
>>> U.name('\ufe54')
'SMALL SEMICOLON'
>>> U.east_asian_width('\ufe54')
'W'
>>> U.east_asian_width('一')
'W'
>>> U.east_asian_width('\ufe53')
'F'
>>> U.east_asian_width('\0')
'N'
>>> U.east_asian_width('\ufffe')
'F'
>>> U.east_asian_width('\ufeff')
'N'

from seed.data_funcs.rngs import make_Ranges, sorted_ints_to_iter_nontouch_ranges, detect_iter_ranges, StackStyleSimpleIntSet, StackStyleSimpleIntMapping, TouchRangeBasedIntMapping
d = StackStyleSimpleIntMapping()
for j in range(0x11_00_00):
    d[j] = U.east_asian_width(chr(j))

>>> d.len_rngs()
1861
>>> sorted({*d.iter_values__per_rng_(reverse=False)})
['A', 'F', 'H', 'N', 'Na', 'W']

w2s = {}
for rng, w in d.iter_rng_value_pairs_(reverse=False):
  s4w = w2s.setdefault(w, StackStyleSimpleIntSet())
  s4w.push_rng(rng)

for w, s4w in sorted(w2s.items()):
    print((w, s4w))
      #输出移至下面:

for w, s4w in sorted(w2s.items()):
    print((w, s4w.len_rngs()))
('A', 179)
('F', 697)
('H', 7)
('N', 846)
('Na', 7)
('W', 125)


j2wc = StackStyleSimpleIntMapping()
for j in range(0x11_00_00):
    ch = chr(j)
    w = U.east_asian_width(ch)
    gc = U.category(ch)
    j2wc[j] = (w,gc)

j2wc.len_rngs()#4318

#(w,gc)共95个:见下面
for w, gc in sorted({*j2wc.iter_values__per_rng_(reverse=False)}):
    print(f'{w}.{gc}')

---

ls4wc = []
for (i,j), (w, gc) in j2wc.iter_rng_value_pairs_(reverse=False):
    sz = j-i
    s = f'{w}.{gc}@0x{i:X}+{sz}'
    k = (w, gc, i)
    ls4wc.append((k,s))

ls4wc.sort()
for k,s in ls4wc:print(s)

with open(r'/sdcard/0my_files/tmp/全角标点-w.gc.begin.sz.txt', 'xt', encoding='ascii') as ofile:
    for k,s in ls4wc:print(s, file=ofile)

---

def show__j2w__F_W_(ofile, __j2w, /):
  for w_ in 'FW':
    for (i,j), w in __j2w.iter_rng_value_pairs_(reverse=False):
      if not w == w_:continue
      for k in range(i,j):
          ch = chr(k)
          nm = U.name(ch)
          gc = U.category(ch)
          print(f'{w}.{gc}@0x{k:X}:{ch}:{nm}', file=ofile)


show__j2w__F_W_(None, __j2w)

with open(r'/sdcard/0my_files/tmp/全角标点-只保留SP-只保留FW.txt', 'xt', encoding='utf8') as ofile:
    show__j2w__F_W_(ofile, __j2w)

[[
vs:
  0x20A9 ₩
  0xffe6 ￦
===

>>> ch=chr(0x20A9)
>>> U.name(ch)
'WON SIGN'
>>> ch
'₩'

>>> ch=chr(0xffe6)
>>> U.name(ch)
'FULLWIDTH WON SIGN'
>>> ch
'￦'

]]
